2025-06-10 14:26:12.619 -08:00 [INF] Executed DbCommand (25ms) [Parameters=[], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT [p].[Id], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[CreateDate], [p].[Image], [p].[Ingredients], [p].[Name], [p].[Price], [c].[Id], [c].[CategoryTypeId], [c].[CreateDate], [c].[Image], [c].[Name], [c0].[Id], [c0].[CreateDate], [c0].[Name], [t].[Id], [t].[CreateDate], [t].[ProductId], [t].[SizeId], [t].[Id0], [t].[CreateDate0], [t].[Name]
FROM [Products] AS [p]
INNER JOIN [Categories] AS [c] ON [p].[CategoryId] = [c].[Id]
INNER JOIN [CategoryTypes] AS [c0] ON [c].[CategoryTypeId] = [c0].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p0].[Id], [p0].[CreateDate], [p0].[ProductId], [p0].[SizeId], [s].[Id] AS [Id0], [s].[CreateDate] AS [CreateDate0], [s].[Name]
    FROM [ProductSizes] AS [p0]
    INNER JOIN [Sizes] AS [s] ON [p0].[SizeId] = [s].[Id]
